overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.497em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.652em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow><mo>(</mo><mfrac><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi></mrow><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mo>)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>(</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>3</mn><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mo>)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>∴</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>4</mn></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-4">\rm \left(\frac{-2+x}{2}\right)=\left(\frac{3-1}{2}\right)\Rightarrow x-2=2\therefore x=4</script></span></p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

clip: rect(3.568em, 1000.37em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -3.686em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.162em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-115" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">a</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.904em, 1000.49em, 1.191em, -999.998em); top: -1.268em; left: 0em;"><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: 0em; border-top: 1.5px solid; width: 0.494em; height: 0px;"></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.068em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.969em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.497em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.602em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>3</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">a</mi></mfrac></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-14">\rm=\frac{3}{a}</script></span></p>

<p><span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-15-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo>&amp;#x2234;</mo><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>&amp;#x00D7;</mo><mfrac><mn>3</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>a</mi></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>&amp;#x21D2;</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>a</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>6</mn></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-116" style="width: 10.781em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 8.814em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.191em, 1008.77em, 2.666em, -999.998em); padding-left: 0.289em;">−</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-120" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-121" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">×</span><span class="mfrac" id="MathJax-Span-122" style="padding-left: 0.207em;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.494em; height: 0px; margin-right: 0.125em; margin-left: 0.125em;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1000.33em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.424em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.162em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-123" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">3</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.568em, 1000.37em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -3.686em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.162em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-124" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">a</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.904em, 1000.49em, 1.191em, -999.998em); top: -1.268em; left: 0em;"><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.497em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.602em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo>∴</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>×</mo><mfrac><mn>3</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">a</mi></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">a</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>6</mn></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-15">\rm \therefore-2\times\frac{3}{a}=-1\Rightarrow a=6</script></span></p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>

                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial"><span>Question 6</span></div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p><span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-49-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>x</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>3</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>y</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>6</mn><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>&amp;#x21D2;</mo><mfrac><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>x</mi><mn>3</mn></mfrac><mo>+</mo><mfrac><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>y</mi><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-505" style="width: 11.232em; <p>রেখাটি x&nbsp;ও y&nbsp;অক্ষকে (3, 0) ও (0, 2) বিন্দুতে ছেদ করবে।</p>

<p><span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-67-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>&amp;#x21D2;</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>y</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>3</mn><mo>=</mo><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><mn>2</mn><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>x</mi><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>&amp;#x21D2;</mo><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>x</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>y</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>3</mn><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-698" style="width: 18.895em;                                         <span style="color: black !important;"><p>যোগ করে,&nbsp;<span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-112-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>x</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>7</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>y</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>3</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>x</mi><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><mn>7</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>y</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>14</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>11</mn></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1451" style="width: 12.256em; <p>বা,&nbsp;<span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-113-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mn>5</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>x</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>25</mn><mo>&amp;#x2234;</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>x</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>5</mn></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1468" style="width: 7.01em; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.148em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.002em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mn>5</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>25</mn><mo>∴</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>5</mn></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-113">\rm 5x=25\therefore x=5</script></span></p>

<p>সুতরাং,&nbsp;<span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-114-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mn>2</mn><mo>&amp;#x00D7;</mo><mn>5</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>7</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>y</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>14</mn></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1478" style="width: 6.764em; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.297em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.153em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mn>2</mn><mo>×</mo><mn>5</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>7</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">y</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>14</mn></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-114">\rm 2\times5+7y=14</script></span>&nbsp;বা,&nbsp;<span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;                                     <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial"><span>Question 17</span></div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>x ও y&nbsp;অক্ষ এবং <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-116-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mn>4</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>x</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>3</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>y</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>6</mn></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1501" style="width: 6.224em; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1559" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">1</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.969em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -1.047em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 2.353em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mn>4</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>3</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">y</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>6</mn><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>4</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi></mrow><mn>6</mn></mfrac><mo>+</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>3</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">y</mi></mrow><mn>6</mn></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi><mfrac><mn>3</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac></mfrac><mo>+</mo><mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">y</mi><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-120">\rm 4x+3y=6\Rightarrow\frac{4x}{6}+\frac{3y}{6}=1\Rightarrow\frac{x}{\frac{3}{2}}+\frac{y}{2}=1</script></span></p>

<p>ক্ষেত্রফল&nbsp;<span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-121-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mo>&amp;#x00D7;</mo><mfrac><mn>3</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mo>&amp;#x00D7;</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>3</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1560" style="width: 7.584em;                 <div class="TakeExamHeader">
                    <h2 style="font-size: 25px;font-weight: bolder;color: #000000;">Written</h2>

            <div class="TakeExamBody">
                        <div class="row questionBlock">
                                                        <div class="row question">
                                <div class="col-md-12" style="padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px;">
                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial"><span>Question 21</span></div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <table border="0" cellpadding="1" cellspacing="1" style="width: 100%;">
	<tbody>
		<tr>
			<td>y অক্ষের ধনাত্মক দিকের সাথে 30° কোণ উৎপন্নকারী ও মূলবিন্দু থেকে 5 একক দূরে অবস্থিত সরলরেখার সমীকরণ এবং সরলরেখাটি দ্বারা y-অক্ষের খন্ডিতাংশের দৈর্ঘ্য নির্ণয় কর।</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: bottom; text-align: right;">২.৫</td>
		</tr>
	</tbody>
</table>

clip: rect(0.904em, 1000.49em, 1.191em, -999.998em); top: -1.268em; left: 0em;"><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: 0em; border-top: 1.5px solid; width: 0.494em; height: 0px;"></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.068em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1956" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1957" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">±</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1958" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">5</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1959" style="font-family: MathJax_AMS; padding-left: 0.289em;">∴</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1960" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">c</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1961" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1962" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">±</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1963" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">10</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 3.035em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.747em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 2.152em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow><mo>|</mo><mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">c</mi><msqrt><mn>3</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></msqrt></mfrac><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>5</mn><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">c</mi><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mo>±</mo><mn>5</mn><mo>∴</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">c</mi><mo>=</mo><mo>±</mo><mn>10</mn></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-147">\rm \left|\frac{c}{\sqrt{3+1}}\right|=5\Rightarrow\frac{c}{2}=\pm5\therefore c=\pm10</script></span></p>

<p><span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-148-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo>&amp;#x2234;</mo></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1964" style="width: 0.658em; <p>এবং y&nbsp;অক্ষের খন্ডিতাংশের দৈর্ঘ্য&nbsp;<span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-150-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>|</mo><mrow><mo>&amp;#x00B1;</mo><mfrac><mn>10</mn><mn>1</mn></mfrac></mrow><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>10</mn></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1979" style="width: 5.863em; font-family: MathJax_Main; top: -3.031em; left: 0em;">∣<span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1984"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1985" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">±</span><span class="mfrac" id="MathJax-Span-1986"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.822em; height: 0px; margin-right: 0.125em; margin-left: 0.125em;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1000.7em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.424em; left: 50%; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.497em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.602em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>|</mo><mrow><mo>±</mo><mfrac><mn>10</mn><mn>1</mn></mfrac></mrow><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>10</mn></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-150">\rm =\left|\pm\frac{10}{1}\right|=10</script></span>&nbsp;একক।</p>

<p><strong>নম্বর বণ্টনঃ</strong></p>

<p><strong><span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-151-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>c</mi><mo>=</mo><mo>&amp;#x00B1;</mo><mn>10</mn></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1992" style="width: 3.609em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.953em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.191em, 1002.91em, 2.133em, -999.998em); top: -1.965em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1993"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1994" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">c</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1995" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1996" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">±</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1997" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">10</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.969em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.098em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.953em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">c</mi><mo>=</mo><mo>±</mo><mn>10</mn></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-151">\rm c=\pm10</script></span></strong>&nbsp;;&nbsp;নির্ণয়ের জন্য ০.৫ নম্বর।</p>

<p><span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-152-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><msqrt><mn>3</mn></msqrt><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>x</mi><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>y</mi><mo>&amp;#x00B1;</mo><mn>10</mn><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1998" style="width: 7.666em; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.076em, 1000.86em, 4.346em, -999.998em); top: -4.055em; left: 0em;"><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">√</span><span style="display: inline-block; padding-left: 0.207em;">−</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-2005" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">y</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-2006" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; <p>y অক্ষের খন্ডিতাংশের দৈর্ঘ্য = 10&nbsp;একক; নির্ণয়ের জন্য ০১ নম্বর।<br>
<strong>[বি:দ্র: একক না লিখলে বা ভুল একক লিখলে ০.৫ নম্বর কর্তন করা হবে।]</strong></p>
